event = {
 id = 62901
 country = ITA
 style = 2
 picture = "militaryparade1"
 decision_picture = "decision_diplomatic_campaign"
 persistent = yes

 decision = {
     control = { province = 29 data = -1 }                # London is controlled by us
     alliance = { country = EUS country = ITA }        # We must be allied to the Carlists
     NOT = { 
         government = communist                             # Not syndicalist
         exists = SCO
         exists = U16                                                # England and Scotland don't exist
         alliance = { country = CAN country = -1 }    # We're not allied to Canada
         alliance = { country = U07 country = -1 }        # We're not allied to the UK
         alliance = { country = GER country = -1 }        # We're not allied to Germany
         war = { country = ENG country = -1 }             # We're not at war with the UoB
     } 
 }

 decision_trigger = {
 }

 trigger = {
     control = { province = 29 data = -1 }                # London is controlled by us
     OR = {
         alliance = { country = EUS country = -1 }
         alliance = { country = ITA country = -1 }        # We must be allied either to the Pope or to the Carlists
     }
